  let halide_upmem_free_result = halide_upmem_free("kernel_0")
  assert(halide_upmem_free_result == 0, halide_upmem_free_result)
 }
}


Module.compile(): c_upmem AOT_result/gemv_generate
dir_rmdir: /tmp/SR1GlG
